[06/11/2022, 2:38:23â€¯PM] ~â€¯Yudhajit Bhattacharjee: okay. tahole send this message to indian groups.

"INFO: *Please do not use DD cargo (https://www.dd-cargo.com/) to ship your stuff from Israel to India*. I was a student at Bar Ilan and sent a box to Kolkata from Tel Aviv, in January. The box has not yet arrived and probably never will. The people at the company often do not respond, and when they do, they make up weird excuses like customs clearance charges have increased and hence we have to wait, or that the parcel is being shipped back to Israel and needs to be shipped again. Eventually they stopped responding after late September. 

There are multiple people complaining in their FB page, but those comments get deleted quickly. So it isn't a one-off situation with me, it is a common occurrence. Hence avoid this company and please spread this message to other Indian groups in Israel warning them. 

~Manuj Mukherjee, Postdoc 2020-2022 @ Bar Ilan"

[24/08/2023, 9:11:19â€¯AM] ~â€¯Ankit: According to Indian patent act section 39, no person residing in India shall make or cause to be made any patent application outside India, unless a patent application for the same invention has already been filed in India, and not less than six weeks have passed. If an inventor wishes to file outside India without filing first in India, the inventor must first obtain a foreign filing license from the India Patent Office.

 

The definition for assessing if the individual would be considered as Resident of India or otherwise:

 

1. Stay in India for a year is 182 days or more (the year would the financial year in which the first Application is being filed) or

 

2. Stay in India for the immediately 4 preceding financial years is 365 days or more and 60 days or more in the relevant financial year.

 

 

The Documentary Requirement for procuring Foreign Filing License:

Â·  Title of the invention.

Â·  Countries in which the proposed applications are to be filed (we usually mention all PCT member countries and all convention countries by default).

Â·  Name, Address and nationality of the assignee, if any.

Â·  Name, address and nationality of the Indian inventors (along with their Indian Addresses).

Â·  Power of Attorney from the Indian inventors mentioning their Indian address (simple signatures needed, legalization/ notarization not needed). We attach hereby our blank template of POA, please fill in the name and address (complete Indian Address with CITY, STATE,COUNTRY and PIN CODE) and get the same executed with handwritten signatures. No legalization/notarization required.

Â·  Name, address and nationality of any non-Indian inventors.

Â·  Complete specification (we may file as much information as is available, preferably if claims and drawings are available, the same should be filed to expedite the process).

 

We also received a cost estimate for obtaining foreign filing license of about EURO 450 â€“ associate charges. The Indian patent office is required to response within 21 days.

*Update from the Technion*

Currently, there are no specific directives from the Home Front Command for the Haifa region.

We remain vigilant and ready. Shelters on campus are now open, and we are in the process of setting up a situation room. The Technion administration is actively monitoring the situation and will provide further updates later today.

We advise downloading the Home Front Command application: https://www.oref.org.il/12487-20626-en/Pakar.aspx.
For immediate assistance, the Security Unit's hotline is available 24/7 at 04-8292222 or https://bitahon.technion.ac.il/.

We'll keep you informed as new information arises.

Technion Update Concerning the Recent Events in the South
Saturday, 7th October 2023, 18:00
Dear Members of the Technion Community,
Early this morning, Israel entered a state of conflict. Our thoughts and prayers are with the victims' families, the inhabitants of southern Israel, and our defense forces.
The Technion administration is vigilantly monitoring the evolving situation and preparing for multiple contingencies. Campus shelters are now accessible, and a situation room has been established to oversee developments.
As of now, the Home Front Command has issued no specific directives for the Haifa region. We continue our operations as usual, exercising appropriate caution.
Please note the following crucial announcements:
â€¢ Based on the Home Front Command's guidance, activities at the Technion campuses in Haifa will resume as usual tomorrow. However, the Sarona campus in Tel Aviv will remain closed.
â€¢ The second period (Moed B) exams of the spring semester and the first period (Moed A) exams of the summer semester, originally scheduled from Sunday, 8th October 2023, through Friday, 13th October 2023, will be postponed. An updated exam timetable will be released by the Office of Undergraduate Studies. Rescheduled dates will fall within the initial two weeks of the semester, set for afternoons and Fridays.
â€¢ A significant number of students have been mobilized for reserve duty. We stand ready to provide them with all necessary support.
â€¢ In light of a marked uptick in cyber-attack warnings, and in collaboration with the National Cyber Directorate and peer academic institutions, the security of the Technionâ€™s systems has been enhanced. Users outside Israel may encounter intermittent disruptions.
â€¢ The Security Unitâ€™s hotline operates around the clock at 04-8292222. More details can be found at https://bitahon.technion.ac.il.
â€¢ The Dean of Students Office remains available to assist. For any concerns, please reach out to:
Adih@technion.ac.il
counseling-director@technion.ac.il
We urge everyone to closely follow and adhere to updates and guidelines disseminated via email, WhatsApp, the Technion website, and our social media platforms.

Overall, there was nothing unusual about getting to Ben Gurion, the security, and all airport procedures.

[13/10/2023, 3:19:36â€¯PM] Sriman: Students who are currently staying abroad or who wish to go abroad due to the war situation are of course entitled to do so. Those who wish to continue their studies from abroad for a limited period of one semester should arrange this by submitting the following documents to the Graduate School via the Graduate School Secretary of their academic unit (this can also be done from abroad): â€¢ A letter of request, including reference to timetables and research milestones.  â€¢ Advisor's recommendation and confirmation that the research may be continued temporarily while abroad. â€¢ For Master's students who are required to take courses â€“ Advisor's approval and Vice Dean approval regarding a feasible possibility for course studies from abroad, or alternatively, submission of a study program that does not include courses during 2023-24 Winter semester. â€¢ Advisor's and Vice Dean's recommendation for awarding a scholarship for the period abroad (if there is an intention to award it). Alternatively, one can request to hold the scholarship payments, or request an academic leave for the entire 2023-24 Winter semester. Such requests will be submitted through the department using the usual protocol and will be processed as quickly as possible. Due to the situation, the restrictions that normally apply to academic leave approvals will be reconsidered. It is important to note that the procedures appearing in this section refer to active students who have already begun their studies. The possibility of aadjusting and applying them to new students who are supposed to begin their studies in the winter semester 2023/2024 but are currently abroad is being examined. Guidelines regarding this option it will be published in the coming days.

[25/10/2023, 4:46:57â€¯PM] ~â€¯Rohith Polisetty: INPUT REQUIRED : Applying for Temporary Workspaces in India for students affiliated to Israeli institutes

Hello Everyone,
Following up on my last message regarding this, I am happy to announce that this issue has been discussed within a govt. scientific agency, and we have been asked to provide further data that can be used to setup communication between the interested students and relevant stakeholders.

I request you to read this message carefully and if you are interested please fill up this form with correct details. Please also circulate this link among your peers.

Just to reiterate, this is for the possibility for finding Indian research groups and educational institutes that may volunteer to offer temporary workspaces, allowing you to continue some of your work. 

This initiative provides an excellent opportunity to maintain a connection with your work  and the potential to develop collaborations with groups in India.
Rest assured, the information provided will be kept secure, and only shared with relevant govt. agencies. Please do not provide any confidential information. Please note that registering here does not guarantee you anything, it depends on a variety of factors to find a suitable match for you in India.

If you have any concerns or queries, please feel free to reach out to me.

Regards,
Rudra Nayan Das (Weizmann Institute of Science)
